actor MMEarthElemental //7290 		//baron of hell
{
	DropItem "Mana1Ammo"
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "PowerslaveSpawner" 28
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
    Health 1000
    Mass 1000
    Radius 20
    Height 56
    Speed 8
    PainChance 75
    Scale 0.28
    Monster	+DONTCORPSE	RipLevelMin 1 
    +FLOORCLIP
//    BloodColor Brown
    +BOSSDEATH
    +NOBLOOD
    +DONTMORPH
	+DONTCORPSE
    MinMissileChance 220
    Obituary "%o was rocked to sleep by an earth elemental."
    MeleeDamage 9
    SeeSound "Golem/Attack"
    PainSound "Golem/Pain"
    DeathSound "Golem/death"
    ActiveSound "CryptDemon/Sight"
    DamageFactor "Wormwood", 0.5
    PainChance "Charm", 96
    PainChance "Terror", 96
    PainChance "Drain", 64
    PainChance "Chaos", 255
    PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 128
    PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 128
//Armor
	DamageFactor "Electric", 1.5
	DamageFactor "Plasma", 0.75
	DamageFactor "PlasmaDisint", 0.75
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 0.5
    States
    {
	Pain.Charm:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
		Goto See
    Pain.Terror:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
		Goto See
    Pain.Drain:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto Pain
    Spawn:
        EREL A 20 A_Look
        Loop
    See:
        EREL BCDEFGHI 3 A_Chase
        Loop
    Melee:
        EREL JK 4 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("Golem/Attack")
        EREL L 4 A_MeleeAttack
        EREL MNOP 4
        Goto See
    Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(256,"M2")
        EREL JK 4 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("Golem/Attack")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("GroundRock2Dust",40,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS)
        EREL L 4 A_SpawnItemEx("GroundRock2",40,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_SETMASTER|SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS)
        EREL MNOP 4
		EREL A 30
		Goto See
	M2:
        EREL JK 4 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("Golem/Attack")
        EREL L 4 A_CustomMissile("GroundSpike",32,0,0)
        EREL MNOP 4
		Goto See
    Pain:
        EREL Q 2
        EREL R 2 A_Pain
        EREL STUV 2
        Goto See
    Death:
        EREL QR 3
        EREL W 3 A_Scream
        EREL XY 3
        EREL Z 3 A_Fall
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
        ERED A -1 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
        Stop
    Ice:
		EREL Q 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
		EREL Q 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		EREL Q 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks
		Wait
    Raise:
        ERED A 3
        EREL ZYXWRQ 3
        Goto See
    Death.UnholyDisint:
    Death.PlasmaDisint:
    Disintegrate:
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		Medium
		)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
    }
}

Actor GroundRock2
{
	+NOINTERACTION
    Projectile 
	+SEEKERMISSILE
    Speed 25
    Damage 15
    Radius 12
    Height 12
    Scale 0.4
    DeathSound "Golem/death"
    States
    {
    Spawn:
		HHRB AAAAAAA 2 ThrustThingZ(0,2,0,1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_Stop
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",0)
		"####" "#" 0 A_TransferPointer(AAPTR_TARGET,AAPTR_DEFAULT,AAPTR_TARGET,AAPTR_TRACER,4) //Set the thrower's target as tracer and seek.
		"####" "#" 0 A_FaceTracer
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeVelocity(cos(-pitch)*25,0,sin(-pitch)*25,CVF_RELATIVE|CVF_REPLACE)
		//"####" "#" 0 A_SeekerMissile(90,90,SMF_PRECISE)
	Moving:
		"####" "#" -1
		Loop
    Death:
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RockSmashedPart1",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RockSmashedPart2",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RockSmashedPart3",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		TNT1 A 1 A_SpawnItemEx("GroundRock2Explo",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION)
		Stop
    }
}

actor MMBoneDragon 7291		//spidermaster
{

    Health 4500
    Radius 64
    Height 88
    Speed 10
    Mass 90000
    PainChance 32
    Scale 0.85
    Monster	+DONTCORPSE	RipLevelMin 1

    +BOSS
    +NORADIUSDMG

    +FLOAT
    +NOICEDEATH

    +NOBLOOD
    +DONTMORPH
    +NOFEAR

    PainSound "diablo2/bighead/pain"

		TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("BoneDragonAnyShotFX",80,0,random(45,-45))
		BDRA M 4 
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("BoneDragonAnyShotFX",80,0,random(45,-45))
		BDRA N 4 
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("BoneDragonAnyShotFX",80,0,random(45,-45))
		BDRA OP 4
		Goto See
    MaelstromAttack:
		BDRA IJ 4 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("BoneDragonAnyShotFX",80,0,random(45,-45))
		BDRA K 4
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("BoneDragonAnyShotFX",80,0,random(45,-45))

		TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("BoneDragonAnyShotFX",80,0,random(45,-45))
		BDRA M 4 
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("BoneDragonAnyShotFX",80,0,random(45,-45))
		BDRA N 4 
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("BoneDragonAnyShotFX",80,0,random(45,-45))
		BDRA OP 4
		Goto See
    Melee:
		BDRA IJ 4 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("BoneDragonAnyShotFX",80,0,random(45,-45))
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/frzshot")
		BDRA KK 1 A_CustomMissile("BlizzardBreathShot",80,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/frzshot")
		BDRA KK 1 A_CustomMissile("BlizzardBreathShot",80,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("BoneDragonAnyShotFX",80,0,random(45,-45))
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/frzshot")
		BDRA LL 1 A_CustomMissile("BlizzardBreathShot",80,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/frzshot")
		BDRA LL 1 A_CustomMissile("BlizzardBreathShot",80,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("BoneDragonAnyShotFX",80,0,random(45,-45))
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/frzshot")
		BDRA MM 1 A_CustomMissile("BlizzardBreathShot",80,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/frzshot")
		BDRA MM 1 A_CustomMissile("BlizzardBreathShot",80,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("BoneDragonAnyShotFX",80,0,random(45,-45))
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/frzshot")
		BDRA NN 1 A_CustomMissile("BlizzardBreathShot",80,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/frzshot")
		BDRA NN 1 A_CustomMissile("BlizzardBreathShot",80,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 AAA 0 A_CustomMissile("BoneDragonAnyShotFX",80,0,random(45,-45))
		BDRA OP 4
		Goto See
    Pain:
        BDRA Q 2
        BDRA R 2 A_Pain
        BDRA STUV 2
        Goto See
    Death:
        BDRA Q 3
        BDRA R 3 A_Scream
        BDRA WXY 3
        BDRA Z 3
		"####" "#" 0 A_UnsetSolid
		BDRA Z 1 A_JumpIf(z <= floorz || abs(velz) <= 0,"Crash")
		Wait
    Crash:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("DisintegrateToken",1,"DisintegrateCont")
		BDRD A 2 A_SetFloorClip
		TNT1 A 0 A_Fall
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		"####" "#" 0 A_QueueCorpse
		BDRD A -1 A_UnSetSolid
		Stop
    Death.UnholyDisint:
    Death.PlasmaDisint:
    Disintegrate:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("DisintegrateToken",1)
    DisintegrateCont:
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		Big
		)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
    }
}

ACTOR	FMaelStromBolt4

	+NOGRAVITY

	+DONTSPLASH

	//	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
		TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_ExtChase(0,0)
	//	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetShootable
		TNT1 AAAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("TelepSmoke1",random(5,40),random(-20,20),0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("misc/teleport")
		MONK A 5 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
    Missile:
		MONK HI 4 A_FaceTarget
		MONK J 4 A_PlaySound("diablo2/vampire/castspell")
		MONK K 0 A_CustomMissile("BaronBall2",44,-7,0)
		MONK K 5 A_CustomMissile("BaronBall2",40,7,0)
		MONK LM 5 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"Teleporting")
		Goto See
    Pain:
        MONK N 2
        MONK O 2 A_Pain
        MONK PQR 2
        Goto Teleport2
    Death:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,7)
        MONK S 4
        MONK T 4 A_Scream
        MONK UV 4
        MONK W 4 A_Fall
		"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
        MONK X -1
        Stop
		TNT1 A 0 A_Die
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RedMiteSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto XDeathBlood
    XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"Defilement")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"XDeathBlood")
		TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_TossGib
		Goto Death
    XDeathBlood:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
    Death.UnholyDisint:
    Death.PlasmaDisint:
    Disintegrate:
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		Medium
		)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
    Raise:
        MONK X 4
        MONK WVUTS 4
        Goto See
    }
}

actor Phoenix //7299		//painelemental
{
	const int ExplosionNormal = 300;
	const int ExplosionFriendly = 2048;
	var int user_friendly;
	var int user_immo;
	var int user_switch;
	var int user_chance;
	var int user_dmg;
	//[0] = Regular damage
	//[1] = Player team damage
	DropItem "PowerslaveSpawner" 48
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
    Health 900
    Radius 20
    Height 56
    Speed 10
    PainChance 32
    Scale 0.28	
    Monster	+DONTCORPSE	RipLevelMin 1 
    +FLOORCLIP
    +NOGRAVITY
    +FLOAT
    +MISSILEEVENMORE
	+NOPAIN
	+NODAMAGE
	+PUSHABLE
	PushFactor 0.1
	Mass 4000
    Obituary "%o was consumed by the phoenix's flames."
    HitObituary "%o was incinerated by the always burning phoenix's claws"
    MeleeDamage 8
    Damage 1000
    SeeSound "phoenix/sight"
    PainSound "phoenix/pain"
    DeathSound "phoenix/death"
    ActiveSound "phoenix/active"
    DamageType Fire
    PainChance "Charm", 0
    PainChance "Terror", 128
    PainChance "Drain", 128
    PainChance "Chaos", 255
    DamageFactor "ChaosExpl1", 0
    DamageFactor "ChaosExpl2", 0
//Fire
	DamageFactor "Fire", 0.5
	DamageFactor "Ice", 1.5
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 1.5
	DamageFactor "AEMagic", 1.5
	DamageFactor "Plasma", 0.75
	DamageFactor "PlasmaDisint", 0.75
    States
    {
	Pain.Charm:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
		Goto See
    Pain.Terror:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
		Goto See

    Spawn:
		PHOX A 0 NoDelay A_SpawnItemEx("PhoenixCountdownMonitor",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_SETMASTER)

		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE",0)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
	Idle:
		PHOX ABCDEFGH 3 Bright A_Look
		Loop
    See:
	Chasing:
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("DONTTHRUST",0)
		PHOX A 0 A_JumpIf(user_friendly == 0,"CE")
		PHOX A 0 A_JumpIf(user_friendly == 1,"CF")
		Goto ChaseCont
	CF: //Chase Friendly
		PHOX A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_friendly",3)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FORCERADIUSDMG",1)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FOILINVUL",1)
		PHOX A 0 A_SetDamageType("TempestLightning")
		PHOX A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_dmg",ExplosionFriendly)
		PHOX A 0 A_CopyFriendliness(AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		Goto ChaseCont
	CE: //Chase Enemy
		PHOX A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_friendly",2)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",0)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FORCERADIUSDMG",0)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FOILINVUL",0)
		PHOX A 0 A_SetDamageType("Fire")
		PHOX A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_dmg",ExplosionNormal)
		PHOX A 0 A_CopyFriendliness(AAPTR_NULL)
		Goto ChaseCont
	ChaseCont:
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE",0)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		PHOX A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_immo",0)
		PHOX AB 3 Bright A_Chase
		PHOX C 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixBurnTrail",random(20,30),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX C 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixSmallDrop",random(10,20),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX CD 3 Bright A_Chase
		PHOX E 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixBurnTrail",random(20,30),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX E 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixSmallDrop",random(10,20),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX EF 3 Bright A_Chase
		PHOX G 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixBurnTrail",random(20,30),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX G 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixSmallDrop",random(10,20),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX GH 3 Bright A_Chase
		PHOX A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixBurnTrail",random(20,30),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixSmallDrop",random(10,20),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX A 0 A_CheckFlag(BUDDHA,1)
		Goto See
		PHOX A 0 A_JumpIf((user_switch == 1) && (health <= 1) && 
			CheckClass("PlayerPawn",AAPTR_TARGET,1),"Alliance")
		Goto See
    Melee:
		PHOX IJ 4 Bright A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixBurnTrail",random(20,30),random(12,-12),0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixSmallDrop",random(10,20),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX K 4 Bright A_MeleeAttack
		PHOX LM 4 Bright
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixBurnTrail",random(20,30),random(12,-12),0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixSmallDrop",random(10,20),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX NO 4 Bright
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixBurnTrail",random(20,30),random(12,-12),0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixSmallDrop",random(10,20),random(12,-12),0)
		Goto See
    Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64,"ImmolationExplosion")
		PHOX IJ 4 Bright A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixBurnTrail",random(20,30),random(12,-12),0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixSmallDrop",random(10,20),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX KKKK 2 Bright A_CustomMissile("DragonFireball2",20,0,0)
		PHOX LM 4 Bright
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixBurnTrail",random(20,30),random(12,-12),0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixSmallDrop",random(10,20),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX NO 4 Bright
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixBurnTrail",random(20,30),random(12,-12),0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixSmallDrop",random(10,20),random(12,-12),0)
		Goto See
    ImmolationExplosion:
		PHOX C 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		PHOX C 0 A_ChangeFlag("DONTTHRUST",1)
		PHOX C 0 A_Stop
		PHOX C 1 Bright A_FaceTarget		//devastating attack, but rare and easy to dodge
		PHOX C 1 Bright A_SkullAttack
	ImmoLoop:
		PHOX CC 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixBurnTrail",random(20,30),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX C 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixSmallDrop",random(10,20),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX C 1 Bright A_CustomMissile("PhoenixBurnTrail",random(20,30),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX C 0 A_JumpIfTargetInsideMeleeRange(1) //A_JumpIfTargetInsideMeleeRange(1)//Closer(70,1)
		Goto ImmoLoop
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("BUDDHA",0)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE",0)
		PHOX A 1 A_Die("MassiveExplosion")
		Goto ImmoDeath
	Alliance:
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		PHOX P 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOTARGETSWITCH",1)
		PHOX P 0 A_SetUserVar("user_dmg",ExplosionFriendly)
		PHOX P 0 A_SetDamageType("TempestLightning")
		PHOX P 0 A_ChangeFlag("FORCERADIUSDMG",1)
		PHOX P 0 A_ChangeFlag("FOILINVUL",1)
	AllegianceSuccessPlayer:
		PHOX P 0 A_RearrangePointers(AAPTR_DEFAULT,AAPTR_DEFAULT,AAPTR_PLAYER1,4)
		PHOX P 0 A_SetUserVar("user_friendly",1)
	AllegianceSuccess:
		PHOX P 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
		PHOX P 3 Bright A_CopyFriendliness(AAPTR_PLAYER1)
		PHOX Q 3 Bright A_Pain
		PHOX R 3 Bright
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixBurnTrail",random(20,30),random(12,-12),0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixSmallDrop",random(10,20),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX STU 3 Bright
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixBurnTrail",random(20,30),random(12,-12),0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixSmallDrop",random(10,20),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX V 2 bright
		PHOX ABCDEFGH 3 bright A_FaceTracer
		PHOX ABCDEFGH 3 bright A_FaceTracer
		PHOX ABCDEFGH 3 bright A_FaceTracer
		PHOX ABCDEFGH 3 bright A_FaceTracer
		PHOX A 0 A_DamageSelf(-900)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("BUDDHA",0)
		PHOX A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_switch",0)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOTARGETSWITCH",0)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		Goto See
    Pain:
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		PHOX P 0 A_SetUserVar(user_immo,0)
		PHOX P 0 A_CheckFlag("FRIENDLY","PCont")
		PHOX P 0 A_CheckFlag("BUDDHA",1)
		Goto TurnOff3
		PHOX P 0 A_JumpIf((health <= 1) && CheckClass("PlayerPawn",AAPTR_TARGET,1),"Alliance")
		Goto TurnOff2
	TurnOff2:
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		PHOX A 0 A_SetUserVar(user_immo,0)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOTARGETSWITCH",0)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE",0)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		Goto PCont
	Turnoff3:
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",1)
		PHOX A 0 A_SetUserVar(user_switch,0)
		PHOX A 0 A_SetUserVar(user_immo,0)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("BUDDHA",0)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOTARGETSWITCH",0)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NODAMAGE",0)
		PHOX A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
		Goto PCont
	PCont:
		PHOX P 3 Bright
		PHOX Q 3 Bright A_Pain
		PHOX R 3 Bright
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixBurnTrail",random(20,30),random(12,-12),0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixSmallDrop",random(10,20),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX STU 3 Bright
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixBurnTrail",random(20,30),random(12,-12),0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixSmallDrop",random(10,20),random(12,-12),0)
		PHOX V 2 Bright
		Goto See
    Death:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("ICECORPSE",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_immo",0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("NoRes",1)
		PHOX P 2
		PHOX Q 2 A_Scream
		PHOX RSTW 2
		PHOX X 2 A_Fall
		PHOX Y 500 CanRaise
		//PHOX Y 0 A_CheckFlag("FRIENDLY",1,AAPTR_MASTER)
		//Goto WaitToRaise
		//PHOX Y 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
		PHOX Y 0 A_TakeInventory("NoRes",1000,0)
	WaitToRaise:
		"####" "#" 0 A_JumpIf(user_friendly == 1 || user_friendly == 3, 2)
		"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(8,2)		//good catch Player701
		PHOX Y 10 CanRaise A_SpawnItemEx("Raiser2",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERPOINTERS|SXF_SETMASTER)
		"####" "#" 0 CanRaise A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		PHOX Y -1 CanRaise
		Stop
	Death.Telefrag:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(health > -500000, "Death")
	Death.MassiveExplosion:
	ImmoDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("IDied",1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_RemoveChildren(1,RMVF_EVERYTHING)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixExplo",20,0,0)			//immolation death
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixExplo2",20,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("PhoenixExplo3",20,0,0)
		TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("TelepSmoke1",random(0,60),random(-60,60),0) //beautiful explosion isnt it? DBT
		TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PhoenixExplPart",0,0,20,random(-10,10),random(-10,10),random(-10,10),random(1,360))
		TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PhoenixExplPart",0,0,20,random(-10,10),random(-10,10),random(-10,10),random(1,360))
		TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PhoenixExplPart",0,0,20,random(-10,10),random(-10,10),random(-10,10),random(1,360))
		TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("PhoenixExplPart",0,0,20,random(-10,10),random(-10,10),random(-10,10),random(1,360))
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySoundEx("weapons/phoenixhit","SoundSlot5")
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("SNDFake1",20,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("SNDFake2",20,0,0)
		TNT1 A 70 A_Explode(user_dmg,2048,XF_NOTMISSILE)
		Stop
	Ice:
		"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(200,"Death")
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("IDied",1)
		"####" "#" 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
		"####" "#" 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks
		Wait
	Death.UnholyDisint:
    Death.PlasmaDisint:
    Disintegrate:
		"####" "#" 0 A_Jump(200,"Death")
		"####" "#" 0 A_GiveInventory("IDied",1)
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		MediumBig
		)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
    Raise:
		PHOX Y 0 A_CheckFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
		Goto EnemyRaise
	FriendlyRaise:
		PHOX Y 0 A_SetUserVar("user_friendly",1)
		Goto RCont
	EnemyRaise:
		PHOX Y 0 A_SetUserVar("user_friendly",0)
		Goto RCont
	RCont:
		PHOX Y 0 A_TakeInventory("NoRes",1000,0)
		PHOX YXW 3 A_ClearTarget
		PHOX Y 0 A_ClearSoundTarget
		PHOX TSRQP 3
		Goto See
    }
}

Actor PhoenixCountdownMonitor
{
	Projectile
	+NOINTERACTION
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(IsPointerEqual(AAPTR_MASTER,AAPTR_NULL),"End")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("IDied",1,"End",AAPTR_MASTER)
		
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(-4500000,"End",AAPTR_MASTER)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower(1,"Reset")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(random(1,256) <= 10,"EnableChance")
		Goto Spawn
	EnableChance:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("PhoenixAlliancePrepOn",1,AAPTR_MASTER)
		TNT1 A 1 A_SetTics(35*random(1,10))
	Reset:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("PhoenixAlliancePrepOff",1,AAPTR_MASTER)
		Goto Spawn
	End:
		TNT1 A 0
		Stop
	}
}

Actor PhoenixAlliancePrepOn : CustomInventory
{
	+INVENTORY.ALWAYSPICKUP
	States
	{
	Pickup:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(CheckClass("Phoenix"),2)
	End:
		TNT1 A 0 A_RailWait
		Stop
		
		TNT1 A 0 A_CheckFlag("FRIENDLY","End")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar(user_switch,1)
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("BUDDHA",1)
		Stop
	}
}

ACTOR Scavenger 7300	//hellknight
{ 
	DropItem "Mana2Ammo"
	DropItem "HealthHeart" 210
	DropItem "PowerslaveSpawner" 28
	DropItem "PowerupSpawner" 8
    Health 600
    Radius 20
    Height 64
    Speed 10
    Mass 500
    PainChance 60
    Scale 0.36
    meleedamage 4
    Monster	+DONTCORPSE	RipLevelMin 1 
    +FLOORCLIP
    SeeSound "diablo2/bighead/sight"
    PainSound "diablo2/bighead/pain"
    DeathSound "diablo2/bighead/death"
    ActiveSound "diablo2/bighead/idle"
    Obituary "O% just was the prey of the scavenger of human sorrow."
    PainChance "Charm", 192
    PainChance "Terror", 192
    PainChance "Defile", 255
    PainChance "Drain", 110
    PainChance "Chaos", 255
    PainChance "ChaosExpl1", 255
    PainChance "ChaosExpl2", 255

//Flesh
	DamageFactor "Electric", 1.5
	DamageFactor "AEPoison", 1.5
	DamageFactor "AEBullet", 2.0
    States
    {
	Pain.Charm:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIENDLY",1)
		Goto See
    Pain.Terror:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("FRIGHTENED",1)
		Goto See
    Pain.Drain:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DrainGiver",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto Pain
    Pain.Defile:
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("DefileCheck",1)
		Goto See
    Spawn:
		M178 Q 1 A_Look
		Loop
    See:
		M178 RST 4 A_Chase
		M178 UVWXY 3 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,2)
		TNT1 A 0
		Loop
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(5,"Death")
		Loop
    Melee:
		M178 QA 2 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("diablo2/bighead/attack")
		M178 BCD 2 A_FaceTarget
		M178 E 2 A_Meleeattack
		M178 FFFGHQ 2 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
    Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128,14)
		M178 QA 2 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("diablo2/bighead/attack")
		M178 BCD 2 A_FaceTarget
		M178 E 2 A_CustomMissile("MMDemonFireBall",32,0,0)
		M178 FFFGHQ 2 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
		M178 LMN 5 A_FaceTarget
		M178 O 0 A_CustomMissile("MMDemonMiniFireBall",40,10,-45)
		M178 O 5 A_CustomMissile("MMDemonMiniFireBall",40,-10,45)
		M178 PQ 5 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
    Pain:
		M178 L 3
		M178 M 3 A_Pain
		M178 NOP 3
		M178 Q 6
		Goto See
    Death:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,6)
		M178 "]" 5
		M178 I 5 A_Scream
		M178 J 5 A_Fall
		M178 K 5 
			"####" "#" 0 A_ChangeFlag("CORPSE",1)
		M178 Z -1
		Stop
		TNT1 A 0 A_Die
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RedMiteSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto XDeathBlood
    XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"Defilement")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"XDeathBlood")
		TNT1 AAAAAAAA 0 A_TossGib
		Goto Death
    XDeathBlood:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("other/gibdeath")
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("BloodGibDropper",0,0,random(20,40),0,0,0,0)
		TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_TossGib
		TNT1 A 1 A_Fall
		Stop
    Death.UnholyDisint:
    Death.PlasmaDisint:
    Disintegrate:
		"----" A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOINTERACTION",1)
		"----" A 0 A_Stop	
		"----" A 0 A_Fall
		"----" A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DisintegrationShadow",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION|SXF_TRANSFERSCALE|SXF_TRANSFERSPRITEFRAME,0,
		MediumBig
		)
		TNT1 A 35
		TNT1 A 0 A_KillMaster("Massacre",KILS_FOILINVUL,None,"AEoDSpawner")
		Stop
    Raise:
		M178 KJI 5
		M178 "]" 5
		Goto See
    }

		TNT1 A 0

		Loop

        M170 I 2 A_Pain
        M170 JK 2
        Goto See

        Goto See

        M170 U 4
        M170 V 4 A_Scream
        M170 W 4
        M170 X 4 A_Fall

        M170 Y -1
        Stop
		TNT1 A 0 A_Die
		TNT1 A 0 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("RedMiteSpawner",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_NOCHECKPOSITION,0)
		Goto XDeathBlood
    XDeath:
		TNT1 A 0 //A_JumpIfInventory("DefileCheck",1,"Defilement")
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(256,"XDeathBlood")
		TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_TossGib
		Goto Death

		Medium
